  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ae7d2029-64cb-4ba3-bb65-b2d6c79ae109'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText15266798517271310434" style="display:none">Anna Whitt, the daughter of a guardian angel and a demon, promised herself she’d never do the work of her father—polluting souls. She’d been naive to make such a vow. She’d been naive about a lot of things. <br /><br />Haunted by demon whisperers, Anna does whatever she can to survive, even if it means embracing her dark side and earning an unwanted reputation as her school’s party girl. Her life has never looked more bleak. And all the while there’s Kaidan Rowe, son of the Duke of Lust, plaguing her heart and mind.<br /><br />When an unexpected lost message from the angels surfaces, Anna finds herself traveling the globe with Kopano, son of Wrath, in an attempt to gain support of fellow Nephilim and give them hope for the first time. It soon becomes clear that whatever freedoms Anna and the rest of the Neph are hoping to win will not be gained without a fight. Until then, Anna and Kaidan must put aside the issues between them, overcome the steamiest of temptations yet, and face the ultimate question: is loving someone worth risking their life?</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/385850276?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ida" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ida" href="/user/show/6418652-ida">Ida</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer385850276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6691362707781845746">Oh Kai, your mind is a very dirty place to be that I have no problem on living in. ;)<br/><br/>Merged review:<br/><br/><b>FIRE! FIRE! FIRE!</b><br/><br/>Call on a battalion of firefighters because I think this book just set my whole being on fire!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386712ra/746336.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Here in our country we are currently experiencing an epic case of heat wave, but dammit, it wasn't the thing that got me sweating an entire ocean! <br/><br/>Seriously, <b>THIS. BOOK. IS. HOTTER. THAN. THE. SUMMER. SUN. </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386712ra/746337.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And I think I just died of heat stroke and went straight up to heaven, because that'</span>
  <span id="freeText6691362707781845746" style="display:none">Oh Kai, your mind is a very dirty place to be that I have no problem on living in. ;)<br><br>Merged review:<br><br><b>FIRE! FIRE! FIRE!</b><br><br>Call on a battalion of firefighters because I think this book just set my whole being on fire!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386712ra/746336.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here in our country we are currently experiencing an epic case of heat wave, but dammit, it wasn't the thing that got me sweating an entire ocean! <br><br>Seriously, <b>THIS. BOOK. IS. HOTTER. THAN. THE. SUMMER. SUN. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386712ra/746337.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I think I just died of heat stroke and went straight up to heaven, because that's the only reason I can think of me feeling this kind of extreme elation!<br><br><br>THIS REVIEW<i><b> MAY CONTAIN SPOILERS</b> </i>FROM THE BOOK(Although the major ones would be hidden), a slight obnoxious amount of VIRTUAL SCREAMING through either means of usage of CAPS or<b> bold letters</b> or <b>BOTH</b> and a heck load of gif pictures of uncontrollable emotions of panic, happiness, fangirling, freaking out and everything and anything in between that cannot be fully expressed by the author. <s>Okay, maybe you've already noticed the caps, bold, and gifs.</s> This long run-on sentence is a proof that you have been warned.<br><br><br>Sweet Peril begins with a prologue about the fate faced by two Nephilim who fell in love with each other in the past. So basically, Wendy Higgins wanted to then and there scare the crap out of all of us, by telling <i>'Yeahhhh...Kaidan and Anna are never ever ever getting back together, unless you want them dead eh?'</i>. Okaaaaaaay, maybe that was just my masochistic(and Taylor Swift song replaying) brain speaking and not what she really meant, but still it was one heck of a downer!<br><br>But be still all fangirl and fanboy hearts, Wendy made up for it big time! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[As in <b>KAIDAN-AND-ANNA-GOT-ALL-STEAMY-AND-SWEATY-AND-OH-MY-GOSH-I-NEED-MULTIPLE-COLD-SHOWERS-NOW</b> time. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <i>*wink*</i><br><br>So after that heartbreaking prologue, this book picks up months after the end of the first book. Anna made a 360 from the school's good girl to this major party girl. But it's all for show, because the demon whisperers are lurking around to see if all the Nephilims are doing their corresponding "jobs".<br><br>But these demon whisperers gave extra attention on breathing down her neck because of the suspicions of some Dukes on her and her father. We then see Anna's struggle on keeping up this facade, that is wholly against her other nature, just to survive. And on top all that, she does this all with a broken heart and other conflicting feelings for a certain boy named Kaidan Rowe.<br><br>Okay, if that was me, I think I might just pass out from all that stress. So, I can't help admire Anna on the way she handled everything that is thrown at her in this book. She handled it with determination and she remained strong all throughout without losing that compassionate side of her that I love. <br><br>But of course, that's not interesting enough, there will be this thing <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[a prophecy about her freeing the Nephilim from the Dukes, and giving chance for the fallen to return to Heaven <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that she unveils which will take her to this trip around the world with Kopano. And thus cue the enter of the love triangle.<br><br>Unlike many love triangles I've read, this has gotta be one of the rare ones that was handled beautifully. Each guy was a given a fair chance<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Or as much as fair chance, Kopano got from Anna <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> with the girl, thus the results and decisions she made was easy to accept and understandable. Each boy got their own special moments with Anna, and Wendy did an amazing job at transitioning the Kopano moments to the Kaidan moments.<br><br>And let's fast forward to those Kaidan moments shall we?<br><br><b>OH DEAR HEAVENS! Excuse me while I faint.</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>OH MY DEAR HEAVENS AGAIN!!!!!!!!! Those Kai moments, were the moments I was living for!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373949ra/727780.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Girls, brace yourselves! Kaidan will get your hormones, ovaries, fallopian tubes and other female parts in a giffy! Heck, he made mine do a tango around my other poor unsuspecting internal organs! I was not kidding when I said that Kaidan and Anna got me sweating. The romantic and sexual tension between this two in this book is unlike anything I have ever witnessed and experienced before. We all witness their blazing chemistry in book 1, but hell fire on loose, this was just a whole other epic level. It's like a flamethrower on steroids with a life of its own, shooting everything in its path and burning them in flames together with this two. It is <b>HOTNESS OVERLOAD</b> with a side of <b>SWOON EXPLOSION</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386712i/746338._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Note: That is still Wade Poezyn, but with long-ish hair. Like the way Kaidan wore it here in Sweet Peril. And yeah, there's Anna. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And yup, there's a scene where they are both in their swinsuit, in the beach side. Hee.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386712ra/746339.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In their time apart and all that denying each other, we can all conclude that there will be a lot of pent up emotion and frustrations. Just imagine that, all breaking out? And yeah, also put that at a limited time frame to deal with. YUP, AN INSTANT SAUNA RIGHT THERE!<br><br>But the main thing that I love most about those moments, aside from the obvious <s>totally hot</s> reasons, is the vulnerability that we got to witness from Kai. He managed to open up, if not all, most of his insecurities and fears to Anna. They developed this honesty in their relationship towards the end and it was just so sweet, and sigh-worthy. And I fell a little more in love with Kaidan Rowe. And I can't even begin to cope how that's possible because I already love him too much. Eeeeepppp!<br><br>Dear Kaidan,<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386712ra/746340.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Love, Me.<br><br>The other characters we love such as the twins, Blake, Patti and Belial was very much present too. Ginger, who I didn't like in the first book, has surprisingly grown on me. Marna was just this perfect best friend for <s>us readers</s>Anna, asking all the right questions to the tidbits we badly want to know! LOL. AND A BIG SHOUT OUT TO BLAKE! This guy is funny as hell and I adore him so much! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I wouldn't mind too if he and Ginger would get a book of their own. ;)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>New characters will also be introduced that would play a vital part in the last book. A particular scene towards the end involving most of them had my heart frozen from the suspense! It was crazy! I felt like I was there with them and all!<br><br>This sequel was a perfect follow-up to a series that is quickly becoming one of best I've read. It provided a great continuation to the main plot and build this strong foundation to a new one that will aid to an already seeming unforgettable finish. It was captivating, thrilling, heart-stopping and just downright amazing. I'm already craving and begging for more! How can I ever wait for another year?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386712i/746341.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>-----<br>Updated 03-16-13<br><br>Just read the first chapter of this book and gaaaaaaaaah! THE FEELS! Someone help my aching heart! I need this book now! *le cries*<br><br>----<br><br><b>KAIDAAAAAAAAAANNNNNNNNNNNNN!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386712i/746342._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386712i/746343._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386713ra/746344.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I JUST NEED MORE OF YOU, OKAY?</b> <i> *lies in a heap under your feet* </i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485168790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17619739207777947508"><b>
  <u>Meet Kaidan Rowe...</u>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401993i/780846.jpg' alt='53da1a21 fb0e 436e 92e6 aeab74ade17d zpsed10de16' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/app.php' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Who is he?</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>The main drummer in a band<br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780847.gif' alt='tumblr loz9is Y6661qd36g7o1 500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/app.php' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Desired by all the girls<br/><br/>Loved by his fans<br/><br/>But he's also an 18 year old boy and the son of Pharzuph, who's the duke of Lust.</b><br/><br/><b>And against the rules, Kaidan fell for a half angel-half demon girl, who's the daughter of Belial - the Duke of substance abuse (e.g alcohol, drugs, etc).</b><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Meet Anna Whitt...</u>
</b><br/> <br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401993i/780848.jpg' alt='556c24c8 c725 4553 9ec7 3e9cf056c25b zps57be01e7' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/app.php' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/><b><u>Who is she?</u><br/><br/>A good 17 year old girl who is turning bad ever since the boy she loved left her. She is struggling to resist the tempt</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17619739207777947508" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Meet Kaidan Rowe...</u>
</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401993i/780846.jpg" alt="53da1a21 fb0e 436e 92e6 aeab74ade17d zpsed10de16" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Who is he?</u>
</b><br><br><b>The main drummer in a band<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780847.gif" alt="tumblr loz9is Y6661qd36g7o1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Desired by all the girls<br><br>Loved by his fans<br><br>But he's also an 18 year old boy and the son of Pharzuph, who's the duke of Lust.</b><br><br><b>And against the rules, Kaidan fell for a half angel-half demon girl, who's the daughter of Belial - the Duke of substance abuse (e.g alcohol, drugs, etc).</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Meet Anna Whitt...</u>
</b><br> <br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401993i/780848.jpg" alt="556c24c8 c725 4553 9ec7 3e9cf056c25b zps57be01e7" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b><u>Who is she?</u><br><br>A good 17 year old girl who is turning bad ever since the boy she loved left her. She is struggling to resist the temptations, but is slowly failing</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780849.gif" alt="tumblr mhcmt9 Ari K1rue90ro1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>She's destined for greatness<br><br>But can she do it without Kaidan? Can she hold on and keep her head in the game? And what of Kopano - the son of Wrath?<br></b><br><i>Sweet Peril</i> is the sequel to <i>Sweet Evil</i>, which i absolutely loved and couldn't put down. This was a fantastic continuation to the trilogy and i was not let down. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780850.gif" alt="tumblr ljlql4 Wem S1qc5xzp" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>I won't tell you what <i>Sweet Peril</i> is about because i don't want to give away any spoilers for the previous book, but i will say this - it's based on teens who's lives literally depend on being bad influences. This is the fate of sons and daughters of the Fallen Angels. Most of them don't have a choice but to do the bidding of their parents, they call it 'working'.<br><br><i>e.g - working, for the son of Lust, is considered having sex and seducing woman. </i><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I was more myself with you during those three days than I’ve ever been with anyone in my life. It’d be easier if I could be fake with you, but you bring out everything in me, little Ann. All of it.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>This book is a solid 5 star read if you ignore my issues with it - like not being able to get into it more because of lack of time. <br><br>I also had an issue with Anna, she was sometimes really annoying and was too good -she didn't let/like when people swore and she stopped Kaidan from saying dirty words to her. I was like...<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780851.gif" alt="tumblr m9lbpif ZNn1r7xovu" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780852.gif" alt="tumblr lp41k3 KMU91qd1k3n" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Speaking of talking dirty, there was a lot more steamy hot scenes in this book than in the previous one, which i was certainly happy about. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780853.gif" alt="tumblr mhffgj D4bk1rxnkxao1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Spend the night with me.” (...)<br>“I’m tired of living like I’m not alive.” He dropped his hands from my face to grip my shoulders. “I’m bloody sick to death of it. I want one night to be alive. With you.” He closed his eyes and leaned his forehead on mine.<br>“Please, Anna. One last night and we’ll go back to being safe again. I need this. I need you.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>But don't get your hopes up that you'll get a lot more of Kaidan and Anna scenes, cause my darling, you won't. In fact, half the book is about them getting back together and forgiving each other for their mistakes ( and believe me there were a lot of mistakes when they were seperate).<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401993i/780854.jpg" alt="time to forgive yourself" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Overall</u>
</b><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401993ra/780855.gif" alt="anigif enhanced buzz 4736 1360291424 7 zps31c6f0" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br> <i>Sweet Peril</i> was an amazing read that i extremly enjoyed. Full of action and new truths that just hit you like a fist in the face. There was lots of new, interesting characters that i fell in love with and can't wait to read more about. Definitely recommend this to <i>Sweet Evil</i> fans. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I love you," I whispered.<br><br>"I've loved you longer," he said.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br> <br><br></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer377201781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14682389093528945763"><a href='http://bewitchedbookworms.com/2013/04/sweet-peril-by-wendy-higgins-the-sweet-trilogy-2.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Read full Review at Bewitched Bookworms </a><br/><br/><a href='http://bewitchedbookworms.com/2013/04/sweet-peril-by-wendy-higgins-the-sweet-trilogy-2.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img alt='Sweet Peril by Wendy Higgins ' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385361i/744221._SX540_.jpg' width='95%' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Heartbreak<br/>By the end of Sweet Evil we were up for a dangerous heartbreak as we all know wondered how Kai and Anna could be together, ever. so, with the beginning of Sweet Peril we are already sad and heartbroken and .. Anna’s pure little heart is no less broken and sad. The whole story of Sweet Evil centers around 2 major important plots and one of them is definitely the epic love between the Demon Son and the Angel Daughter. Evil and Pure – how can t</span>
  <span id="freeText14682389093528945763" style="display:none"><a href="http://bewitchedbookworms.com/2013/04/sweet-peril-by-wendy-higgins-the-sweet-trilogy-2.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Read full Review at Bewitched Bookworms </a><br><br><a href="http://bewitchedbookworms.com/2013/04/sweet-peril-by-wendy-higgins-the-sweet-trilogy-2.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="Sweet Peril by Wendy Higgins " src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385361i/744221._SX540_.jpg" width="95%" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Heartbreak<br>By the end of Sweet Evil we were up for a dangerous heartbreak as we all know wondered how Kai and Anna could be together, ever. so, with the beginning of Sweet Peril we are already sad and heartbroken and .. Anna’s pure little heart is no less broken and sad. The whole story of Sweet Evil centers around 2 major important plots and one of them is definitely the epic love between the Demon Son and the Angel Daughter. Evil and Pure – how can they be together? This is what we desperately want to figure out ourselves and I warn you know – tears will fall, hearts will break. And I am not just talking about Anna and Kai because my little heart just felt with them!<br><br>Anna – the pure little Angel-Demon …<br>While Anna was completely innocent in Sweet Evil she now has to start “working” for her Dad so keep up appearance and to fool all the other Dukes and Demons. And we must admire Anna strength and strong will because behaving like this feels totally out fo context for her. But Anna grows and I think we see a remarkable change in Anna. She appears even stronger, more determined than ever and even goes totally out of her comfort zone. I cannot help but admire this girl!! I loved Anna so much already in Sweet Evil – but I love her even more fiercely in Sweet Peril! She combines perfectly her Angel and demonic heritance and becomes a little more edgy <br><br>Sex on Legs or… Kai !<br>Ok I know I shouldn’t associate Sex On Leg with a YA novel, but I just cannot help it when talking about Kaidan Rowe. This sexy demon-son is everything I love in a bad boy – he’s incredibly sexy, mega hot, he can be a total jerk (and yes, especially in Sweet Peril we see a lot of his jerkiness!!) but he has a heart and as much as he doesn’t want his heart to take over, we can see and we love him for this even more! Kai – sexy, dangerous and so sooo stubborn and with a heart he only opens up for Anna, how can we not love him??<br><br>Love and Danger ….<br>One of the main storylines followed Anna’s search for Allies around the world. I loved this part so much! It not only brought us to different places but also introduces a wonderful supporting character we all will love so much – Kopano – Son of Wrath who helps and support Anna on her journey! What seems to be obvious from the synopsis is the introduction of a Love Triangle. But fear not, Wendy Higgins deals so delicately and perfectly with it, that it doesn’t truly hurt, but was completely genuine and understandable! You can only be pushed so much… right? This whole sequel was just amazing, full of love, passion, danger and heartbreak. Girls who easily cry just like me will most definitely shed a tear or two….<br><br>Personal Note: I can't begin to say how much this books means to me. Wendy named one character in one cute scene after 3 of us bloggers. Me, Jenny and Tara and you wouldn't believe, but I had tears in my eyes when I read the scene... I'm a blond girl , Daniela with an European accent!!gosh that was the most amazing feeling ever!!!<br><br>I love Wendy!!<br>Oh and.... Kai...;-))<br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="14682389093528945763" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer401740555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11899706973820990356"><br/><u>
  <i>Initial Reation:</i>
</u><br/><br/>This book should never be a consideration, just a definite yes, yes, and YES. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389230ra/750248.gif' width='240' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Give The Sweet Evil trilogy a chance. The first book did not disappoint and imagine just how freaking unbelievable this one is going to be!? <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389230ra/750249.gif' width='240' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Yeah, I know! I'm rooting for Wendy Higgins and all my favourite characters here :) Get it, girl!<br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Review</u>
</b><br/><br/>This book could have been better. I say this because <i>Sweet Evil</i> was the book that I pimped everywhere. I can't say that I will be doing the same with <i>S</i></span>
  <span id="freeText11899706973820990356" style="display:none"><br><u>
  <i>Initial Reation:</i>
</u><br><br>This book should never be a consideration, just a definite yes, yes, and YES. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389230ra/750248.gif" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Give The Sweet Evil trilogy a chance. The first book did not disappoint and imagine just how freaking unbelievable this one is going to be!? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389230ra/750249.gif" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Yeah, I know! I'm rooting for Wendy Higgins and all my favourite characters here :) Get it, girl!<br><br><b>
  <u>My Review</u>
</b><br><br>This book could have been better. I say this because <i>Sweet Evil</i> was the book that I pimped everywhere. I can't say that I will be doing the same with <i>Sweet Peril</i> because Wendy Higgin's second instalment wasn't as strong as her debut. <br><br>Sweet Peril takes off where its predecessor left and we're back with Anna and her daily Nephlim grind. She's got to work to keep her dad off of the other Duke's radar, turning the human population towards alcohol and drugs, but her heart isn't in it. Partly because she's half angel, and also because Anna's predominantly occupied with thoughts of Kaidan, missing him. They are still trying to take down the Dukes and gather allies, but it felt like all that really mattered was how much Anna missed "Kai." The fate of the world rests in her hands, and all Anna really wanted to do was see the boy. <br><br>To be fair, she does take the responsibility of saving Neph and Humankind seriously, but the teen swoony romance could have been dialled down. They are in love, I get that, but it felt like their romance dominated <b>most</b> of the book. I was looking forward to reading more of Kaidan and Anna, but with the way it was handled in <i>Sweet Peril</i>, I began to tire of their romance. It was like her life basically revolved around him, and one can only read about how smouldering a guy is before it gets to be enough. There are issues with Kopano, as can be expected, as well as an interesting revelation that has to do with Neph and their badges, but in all honesty Sweet Peril had more to do with Kaidan and Anna not being together than anything else. <br><br>I expected more substance, and even though we meet more of the other Neph, discovering additional information in regards to the prophecy, I wasn't as enamoured this time around. The series is still fantastic, I love you Wendy, but I'm hoping that <i>Sweet Reckoning</i> will more than make up for where this book fell short.<br><br><b>3.5/5 stars: Sweet Peril is compelling, and while it picks up nicely from where the former left off, this book fails to deliver as emotional an impact as the first.</b> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11899706973820990356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_376244170" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/376244170" />
    <a title="Taschima" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2435020-taschima"><img alt="Taschima" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574541558p2/2435020.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/376244170?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taschima" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taschima" href="/user/show/2435020-taschima">Taschima</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer376244170" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14114549389166599246"><i>"Traveling the world in search of possibly hostile Neph and eluding murderous Dukes seemed like a piece of cake in comparison to trying to be a good girl in the arms of Kaidan Rose"</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385209ra/744060.gif' width='300' height='170' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Holy damn. Sweet Mercy is what this book should have been called. I am not going to lie, this is a hot piece of novel. Be beware: this book is prone to make the person reading take short and shallow breaths. But there are as many cons as there are pros, sad to say.<br/><br/>Let's get the cons out of the way first. Big con? The </span>
  <span id="freeText14114549389166599246" style="display:none"><i>"Traveling the world in search of possibly hostile Neph and eluding murderous Dukes seemed like a piece of cake in comparison to trying to be a good girl in the arms of Kaidan Rose"</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385209ra/744060.gif" width="300" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy damn. Sweet Mercy is what this book should have been called. I am not going to lie, this is a hot piece of novel. Be beware: this book is prone to make the person reading take short and shallow breaths. But there are as many cons as there are pros, sad to say.<br><br>Let's get the cons out of the way first. Big con? The ending. I felt like the book ended not on a cliffhanger but on the wrong page. Like we needed at least 30-50 pages more to settle the characters in the next stage instead of leaving us midway through. Not cool. I didn't feel like my heart was being ripped away from me (like the first book's ending) but I also didn't feel like it was an ending. Just, another chapter. Another thing was the plot a bit shallow. As deep as a kiddie pool. I can't lie, doesn't mean I didn't devour the novel (I did) but I can still point out where it felt short. The whole book's time span was a year and some months. We went through Anna's senior year like it didn't matter, because I get for the story it didn't but it was still weird. How did this girl graduate anyways? Who knows with all the pretend partying she was doing and the not caring about her school life anymore. It all went by so fast, nothing of her "old life" was really explored. Her old friends were basically pushed to a corner and most of the time she was being all mopie about not having Kai with her (though I can <i>completely</i> understand).<br><br>Which brings us to the PROS. Number one, front and center, being Kaidan.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385209i/744061._SY540_.jpg" width="252" height="336" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385209ra/744062.gif" width="320" height="176" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hellooooo handsome!! Yes, that is my Kaidan too. The scenes between him and Anna are not for the faint of heart. Let's give you a small, tiny, example:<br><br><i>"Kaidan took a predatory step toward me and I instinctually stepped back. In that slow way he stalked forward until I was agaisnt the sink. The intensity of his face charged me, and I swore to myself I'd kill any creature that tried to come between us this time. His hands reached out and gripped the sink on either side of my waist, and without a word his hot mouth covered mine."</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385209ra/744063.gif" width="300" height="166" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It felt like more than half the book was filled with these hot steamy scenes. Which I was definitely not complaining about!<br><br>I wanted to learn more about Blake, he is my second favorite. Maybe we could get a side story from him or something? God I hope so. All the old pals were here too, the twins, Kope, etc. I like all the side characters, they add a lot to the story.<br><br>So yes Sweet Peril was a good continuation! It has it's flaws true, but you certainly get what you are looking for between the pages. Anna wasn't as much of a good girl, which was a plus. Kaidan was as devastatingly gorgeous, and Wendy made half the book a big make out fest. What more can a girl ask for?! Guilty pleasure? Perhaps, but I am enjoying every second of it.<br><br>My last wish: can we get that whole day in Kaidan's apartment from Kai's POV? PLEASE?!?!<br><br>-•-<br><br><a href="http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/03/sweet-peril-sequel-to-sweet-evil-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Click HERE for 4 Yummy Teasers from Sweet Peril!!!</a><br><br>YOWSA! Kai is HOTTER than ever *.*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385209ra/744064.gif" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>UPDATE 9/21/2012<br><br>It has been picked up for publication by HarperTeen!!!! Smart fellows!<br><br>Dreams do come true!<br><br>--<br><br>Wait a second, not picked up for publication? BULLSHIT. I say that if the publishers don't pick up this book for publication (and if they don't they are being the less bright crayons in the box) the author should self publish it, if anything. I'll sure as hell buy it and I am sure a lot of other people will too (just don't leave us hanging. I am EAGERLY waiting for Sweet Hope).</span>
  <a data-text-id="14114549389166599246" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/449158416?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Victoria Scott" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Victoria Scott" href="/user/show/4658088-victoria-scott">Victoria Scott</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449158416" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17025217189898709504">There are very few trilogies in which the second book is as strong as the first. Even fewer where the second book blows the first book to kingdom come. Well, folks, SWEET PERIL plants Wendy Higgins's series firmly in the latter category. <br/><br/>Knowing full well that SWEET EVIL was one of my favorite paranormal romance novels, I knew Higgins had her work cut out if she wanted to impress this girl--but impress she did. SWEET PERIL is chock full of steaminess, excitement extraordinaire, and an ending pow</span>
  <span id="freeText17025217189898709504" style="display:none">There are very few trilogies in which the second book is as strong as the first. Even fewer where the second book blows the first book to kingdom come. Well, folks, SWEET PERIL plants Wendy Higgins's series firmly in the latter category. <br /><br />Knowing full well that SWEET EVIL was one of my favorite paranormal romance novels, I knew Higgins had her work cut out if she wanted to impress this girl--but impress she did. SWEET PERIL is chock full of steaminess, excitement extraordinaire, and an ending powerful enough to have me on my knees begging for the final book. I don't know how you do it, Wendy, but stick a fork in me--because my ass is spent. <br /><br />*applauses* </span>

<div id="review_396865856" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/396865856" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/396865856?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer396865856" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5927215468765508975"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388460i/748975.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>I was amazed by writing, captivated by story and mesmerized by characters. I LOVED IT! This book is about love and hatred, hope and despair, sins and humanity. Sweet Peril is much more than just ordinary paranormal story. Without exaggerating I can say that this series is definitely the best one when it comes to fallen angels (or angels in general) stories!</b><br/><br/>My Kaiden:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388460i/748976._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>My Anna:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379774662i/332526.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Anna is not this naive girl we knew in previous book anymore. Story is set couple of months after events in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11808950.Sweet_Evil__The_Sweet_Trilogy___1_' title='Sweet Evil (The Sweet Trilogy, #1) by Wendy Higgins' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Evil</a>, Ann</span>
  <span id="freeText5927215468765508975" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388460i/748975.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>I was amazed by writing, captivated by story and mesmerized by characters. I LOVED IT! This book is about love and hatred, hope and despair, sins and humanity. Sweet Peril is much more than just ordinary paranormal story. Without exaggerating I can say that this series is definitely the best one when it comes to fallen angels (or angels in general) stories!</b><br><br>My Kaiden:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388460i/748976._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>My Anna:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379774662i/332526.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anna is not this naive girl we knew in previous book anymore. Story is set couple of months after events in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11808950.Sweet_Evil__The_Sweet_Trilogy___1_" title="Sweet Evil (The Sweet Trilogy, #1) by Wendy Higgins" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Evil</a>, Anna is under constant supervision of demon whisperers and she is forced to work for her demon father - she had to become the famous party girl and temp people into commiting sins. Is she happy about it? Of course not, but if she wants to live, she has no other choice. Under weight of guilt and responsibility, it is visible that our little Anna matured up. And I have to admit I love this new version of Anna even better. <br><br>Even after prologue itself, it was clear that this sequel was destined to be more dangerous and depressive than previous book in series. Things were still not looking good at all for Anna and Kaiden or other Nephs. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"My life was a tiny dot on the map. But even those tiny dots could make a difference - especially when they came together. I grasped that thread of hope and let it lift me."</b>
</blockquote><br>Kaiden is still this same tortured soul, feeling unworthy of Anna, pushing her away with every opportunity. But no matter how much he tries to pretend, it is visible how deep his feelings for Anna are. Kaiden is great character. He has hard life, he has none saying in it, but he still tries to be better person even though it seems there is no hope for him to reach happiness. He is admirable and inspiring person. <br><br>Also, even though this is YA series, it has some serious sexy hot feel into it. And I blame it all (in a very good way) on Kaiden. He is just irresistible, sensual and incredibly attractive boy. However, besides Anna's and Kaiden's personal turmoils, Sweet Peril reveals plenty of new info about fallen angels or Nephs and overall it is pretty adventurous story. You will never be bored, on the contrary, you will always be on your toes while reading it.<br><br>Sweet Peril felt like a very mature read to me considering it is categorized as YA genre. Author never idealized characters or life itself and showed negative sides of it in quite believable way even though this is paranormal series we are talking about. And I loved everything about it, there was no single moment I would feel annoyed or bored. Kudos to the author, I seriously cannot wait for final instalment of this trilogy!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388460i/748977.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>

<div id="review_376517330" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/376517330" />
    <a title="eileen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7208929-eileen"><img alt="eileen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514181905p2/7208929.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/376517330?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="eileen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="eileen" href="/user/show/7208929-eileen">eileen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7208929-eileen?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7208929-eileen?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer376517330" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8939841118249523278"><b>Check out more of my reviews at <a href='http://eileenlisblog.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>***Singing and Reading in the Rain***</a>!</b><br/><br/>After the big kaboosh that was Sweet Evil, you expect Sweet Peril to be even a bigger kaboosh, or at least not fall prey to Second Book Syndrome. Luckily, Sweet Peril did all of those things.<br/><br/>Anna Whitt, our protagonist, resident nice, innocent girl, is surprisingly not what I expected her to be. Yes, I read the first book and I got a fair glimpse of who she was as a person, but her innocence act eventually started to make me w</span>
  <span id="freeText8939841118249523278" style="display:none"><b>Check out more of my reviews at <a href="http://eileenlisblog.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">***Singing and Reading in the Rain***</a>!</b><br /><br />After the big kaboosh that was Sweet Evil, you expect Sweet Peril to be even a bigger kaboosh, or at least not fall prey to Second Book Syndrome. Luckily, Sweet Peril did all of those things.<br /><br />Anna Whitt, our protagonist, resident nice, innocent girl, is surprisingly not what I expected her to be. Yes, I read the first book and I got a fair glimpse of who she was as a person, but her innocence act eventually started to make me want to gag and spit. I mean, who's really that nice, full of empathy , and innocent? Also while being the daughter of the Duke of drugs and alcohol? I can understand her wanting too remain with all morals intact, but the way she acted over the littlest things...it just didn't work. Anna constantly went on about how she needed to be good and how she couldn't be any different from her usual pure self. Oh my God, please give me a break. These days, the odds of a teen being that perfect is unheard of. Especially when she's in love with a guy like Kaidan.<br /><br />Aside from that, everything else was phenomenal. Kaidan, especially. Can I just gush and gush and gush over how fantastic he is as a character? He's your typical bad boy, and he is such a grapefruit. No, you didn't hear me wrong. He is a grapefruit. I have an explanation though! Because I had just eaten a red grapefruit and finished Sweet Peril moments before, my mind was a little cloudy. As I was thinking of how I could describe Kaidan to a friend, grapefruit just popped into my mind so I used it. Because that particularly grapefruit was red, like the color of Lust, which is Kaidan's sin. In addition, grapefruits are sweet yet kind of sour, which is exactly Kaidan's personality, if you translate those qualities into human traits.<br /><br />Sweet Peril is the perfect read for those who are fans of romantic tension. With a character like Kaidan, who's hot and sexy and can drive a girl mad, you can't really expect any less can you? The scenes between Anna and Kaidan are both hot yet totally adorable. Although you don't see Kaidan until at least halfway through, Wendy Higgins has a way of successfully transitioning you to that part without losing too much of your interest. Then when he actually shows up, you better get some fans ready for a swoon overload. The way that Wendy delivers on the Kai/Anna scenes is reminiscent of a guilty pleasure. It's enough to take in moderation, but you still crave it whenever you can't eat that food. Which is exactly what you could call Kai. A guilty pleasure.<br /><br />Oozing with romantic tension, a hot YA book boy, and everything that made Sweet Evil fantastic, Sweet Peril doesn't disappoint in the slightest. Fans everywhere will enjoy Wendy Higgins' latest novel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8939841118249523278" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18354548322163896558"><i>'"I need you to be serious."<br/><br/>His blue eyes scorched me. "Oh, I've never been more serious." "I've no clue what you mean."<br/><br/>Oh, <b>his voice.</b><br/><br/>"I'm serious," I said, hoping I sounded stronger than I felt. <br/>We have unfinished business, Kai."<br/><br/>He turned my head back to face him and breathed his next words against my mouth.   <span id="freeText18354548322163896558" style="display:none"><i>'"I need you to be serious."<br><br>His blue eyes scorched me. "Oh, I've never been more serious." He leaned his face down to mine, and I wrenched my head to the side.<br>"You're trying to distract me."<br>His lips skimmed my neck. "I've no clue what you mean."<br><br>Oh, <b>his voice.</b><br><br>"I'm serious," I said, hoping I sounded stronger than I felt. <br>We have unfinished business, Kai."<br><br>He turned my head back to face him and breathed his next words against my mouth. "Oh I'd say we have quite a bit of unfinished business, little Ann."</i><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/203/holyshitty.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387729ra/747903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>This was one addictive book.<br><br>To prove how hooked I am, I give you...<br><b>Booknut's Totally Awesome Playlist of Sweet Peril Songs</b>!!<br><br><u>Parties Hosted/Attended by Anna:</u><br>-	Here We Go Again by Pixie Lott<br>-	All Night Longer (Clean Version) by Sammy Adams<br>-	Bad Influence by P!nk<br><br><u>Kaiden:</u><br>-	Can’t Forget You by The Darkest Days<br>-	Goodbye to the Girl by David Cook<br>-	Incomplete by the Backstreet Boys<br>-	Drive By by Train<br>-	I Don't Wanna Be In Love by Good Charlotte<br>-	Animal by Conor Maynard<br><br><u>Anna:</u><br>-	Bad Intentions by Digital Daggers<br>-	State of Grace by Taylor Swift<br>-	Alive by Leona Lewis<br><br><u>Kaiden and Anna</u>:<br>-	We'll Be A Dream by We the Kings ft. Demi Lovato<br>-	Cowboys &amp; Angels by Dustin Lynch<br>-	Distance by Christina Perri<br><br><u>Marna &amp; Ginger</u>:<br>-	I Love It by Icona Pop<br><br><u>Kope</u>:<br>-	I Can't Not Love You by Every Avenue<br>-	Mr Brightside (Cover) by Masketta Falls<br><br>Overall, <i>Sweet Peril</i> is a great second book to the series - no cliffhangers, no <s>long term</s> heart attacks, and plenty of swooning!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12652820409504726493"><b>Rating: 5 Stars<br/><br/>My Opinion of This Book: I loved it!<br/>___________________________________________</b><br/><br/><b>
  <u>THE GOOD.</u>
</b><br/>⚫<b>Anna</b> Anna has grown so much. In Sweet Evil, she was so innocent, but in this one, we see a whole different side of her. We see this party girl that's so kickass and can defend herself. She's not this weak, naive girl anymore. This Anna is strong. I loved her.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"My girlfriend is a party-angel who can kick some arse and cook."<br/>~Kaidan </i>
</b> <br/><br/>●<b>Kaiden:</b> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424306008i/13743543._SY540_.jpg' width='270' height='360' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Kaidan is as charming as ever, if not even mor</span>
  <span id="freeText12652820409504726493" style="display:none"><b>Rating: 5 Stars<br><br>My Opinion of This Book: I loved it!<br>___________________________________________</b><br><br><b>
  <u>THE GOOD.</u>
</b><br>⚫<b>Anna</b> Anna has grown so much. In Sweet Evil, she was so innocent, but in this one, we see a whole different side of her. We see this party girl that's so kickass and can defend herself. She's not this weak, naive girl anymore. This Anna is strong. I loved her.<br><br><b>
  <i>"My girlfriend is a party-angel who can kick some arse and cook."<br>~Kaidan </i>
</b> <br><br>●<b>Kaiden:</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424306008i/13743543._SY540_.jpg" width="270" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Kaidan is as charming as ever, if not even more. In this one, he's not so scared and he realizes a lot of things and opens up instead of keeping everything locked in like he did in the first novel. He's probably my favorite character in this series.<br><br><b>
  <i>I tried to warn you,<br>but girls never listen.<br>Got your innocence insured?<br>'Cause it's 'bout to be stolen<br>Right out from under your nose.<br>Prepare to curl your toes.<br>I've got a one-track mind.<br>You've got a nice behind.<br><br>Chorus:<br>I had a good thing goin'<br>All numb in my shell,<br>Then you took me by surprise <br>and now I'm scared as hell.<br>I don't wanna feel for you,<br>I don't wanna feel.<br>If feeling means hurting,<br>then I don't wanna be real.<br><br>You crank up my lust, girl,<br>you tame down my rage.<br>You let your inner vixen <br>Roam out of her cage.<br>The moment our lips met<br>I saw it in your eyes,<br>But you were seeing me, too,<br>I now realize.<br><br>Chorus<br><br>What do I want from you?<br>I want everything. <br>And I'm not gonna share ---<br>This ain't a casual fling.<br>You can be my bad girl,<br>I'll even be your good boy. <br>How'd the tables get turned?<br>F*** it, I'll be your love toy.<br><br>Chorus </i>
</b><br><br>⚫<b>The Side Characters:</b> The side characters were pretty cool as well, especially Blake. Blake is so hilarious, I love him. Ginger and the rest of them were awesome too.<br><br>⚫<b>The Romance:</b> The romance was so good. It was the perfect amount. And, well, my OTP is the best. I ship Kai and Anna so much more now. Kanna? I dunno..they need a ship name. <br><br>⚫<b>The Writing:</b> The writing was gorgeous. It's even better than it was in the first book. There's more variety of words and it's more descriptive.<br><br>⚫<b>The Ending:</b> The ending was incredible, it definitely will make you want the next book ASAP.<br><br><b>
  <u>THE BAD.</u>
</b><br>⚫<b>Kope: </b> I don't know, I just feel like his character is a bit bland and he's really awkward.<br><br>⚫There wasn't much of Jay in this book which makes me a bit sad since I really love his character. Hopefully there's more of him in the next book. *crosses fingers*<br><br>⚫<b>Slow Pace (sometimes):</b> Some parts were a bit slow and I found myself being bored (mostly the beginning). <br><br><b>
  <u></u>
</b><br>I don't think this one is as good as the first, but it was still really good. I'm excited to read the next book!<br><br></span>

<div id="review_1165675655" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1165675655" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1165675655?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=owned-physical-copy">owned-physical-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1165675655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16043592623393358331"><i>
  <b>"You bring out everything in me, little Ann. All of it."</b>
</i> <br/><br/><b>What went wrong?</b><br/><br/>While the first book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11808950.Sweet_Evil__The_Sweet_Trilogy___1_' title='Sweet Evil (The Sweet Trilogy, #1) by Wendy Higgins' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Evil</a> was phenomenal, Sweet Peril seemed to be sort of a letdown. I don't know what to think. There was just too much going on in this book but most of those things are not important I don't think they should be included. The plot progression was a bit frustrating. And the first half was also a bit slow.<br/><br/>Apart from that, I find the forced love triangle quite unnecessary. Don't get me wrong. I lo</span>
  <span id="freeText16043592623393358331" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"You bring out everything in me, little Ann. All of it."</b>
</i> <br /><br /><b>What went wrong?</b><br /><br />While the first book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11808950.Sweet_Evil__The_Sweet_Trilogy___1_" title="Sweet Evil (The Sweet Trilogy, #1) by Wendy Higgins" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Evil</a> was phenomenal, Sweet Peril seemed to be sort of a letdown. I don't know what to think. There was just too much going on in this book but most of those things are not important I don't think they should be included. The plot progression was a bit frustrating. And the first half was also a bit slow.<br /><br />Apart from that, I find the forced love triangle quite unnecessary. Don't get me wrong. I love Kopano but I don't think he needs to be a love interest, too. <br /><br />Aaaaand! Anna Whitt. Omg what happened to this sweet and likeable girl in the first book? Her obsession with Kaidan was too overbearing here. <br /><br /><br />*breathes heavily*<br /><br />I don't like girls who are soooo obsessed with a guy. And Anna was just that kind of girl in this book. :( She even had the tendency to be easily affected whenever Kaidan is around and I guess that's my major issue here. <br /><br />Kaidan, on the other hand, was quite a jerk-- well, most of the time. His constant avoiding games irritated me. I don't like what he was doing to Anna during the first parts of this book. Thankfully, he was able to come to his senses during the later part. Still, I am not a fan of his behavior in this book.<br /><br />But anyways, some parts of this book are otherwise interesting. The introduction of new characters like Zania and Caterina, the epic prologue, and Blake and Flynn's amusing personalities.<br /><br />As a whole, this book is not so good for me. But it's not bad either. I still found myself enjoying some parts of it. :)<br /><br />Rating: 3 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="16043592623393358331" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer441995997" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15538671490633419029"><b>Holy. Mother. of. Heavens. </b><br/><br/>I'm officially addicted to this series. I sigh for Kai. I love Kaidan Rowe. This hot fallen angel drummer is absolutely swoon worthy. I have a new guilty pleasure and I feel so dreamy. I'm such a hopeless romantic. <br/><br/>Anyways, <i>Sweet Peril</i> is a great sequel. Anna becomes the good-girl-gone-bad by partying and drinking to please the demon whisperers because it's one way to survive. As a daughter of Substance abuse, she has to work by promoting the sins to people. It's also </span>
  <span id="freeText15538671490633419029" style="display:none"><b>Holy. Mother. of. Heavens. </b><br /><br />I'm officially addicted to this series. I sigh for Kai. I love Kaidan Rowe. This hot fallen angel drummer is absolutely swoon worthy. I have a new guilty pleasure and I feel so dreamy. I'm such a hopeless romantic. <br /><br />Anyways, <i>Sweet Peril</i> is a great sequel. Anna becomes the good-girl-gone-bad by partying and drinking to please the demon whisperers because it's one way to survive. As a daughter of Substance abuse, she has to work by promoting the sins to people. It's also a way of not to think Kaidan Rowe but she couldn't get him out of her mind. She received a message/prophecy from an angel that the fallen angels had a second chance. It's like building an army against the Dukes. To achieve that, she needs trusted allies. She travels with Kopano to find other Nephilims who can support them in the rebellion. It is very a risky, difficult task but Anna must do this in order to get freedom from everything. (So she could love Kaidan freely without worrying demon whisperers &amp; The Dukes)<br /><br />I love how it focuses more on the conflict of the story than the romance aspect. Not that there is no romance in this book. I love how it introduces us to other characters like Kopano, Blake, Zania, Flynn, Ginger &amp; Marna. etc. Emphasizing their characters gives us an opportunity to getting to know their backgrounds and importance of their roles. There are parts that we might missed Kai, but it's really worth the wait. Hahaha! Patience is all you need. ;)<br /><br />I really like Anna's character development on this book. She's more confident, mature and got the angst. Of course we will not forget Kaidan and Anna's love story. There's a little love triangle in this book, but that's only temporary of course. I must say the love story between them is steamier than the first installment. <b>THAT KITCHEN SCENE. ALL THE COOKING. THE BROWNIES OH.MY.GOD. </b> Steamy. Steamy. Steamy. Kaidan is more swoon worthy. He's so sweet, loving, caring, hot and romantic guy. Shizzzzzzzz!! <br /><br />Overall, I love this and I can't wait to read the next one. I NEED MORE KAIDAN!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15538671490633419029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Summer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Summer" href="/user/show/14778159-summer">Summer</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer582529204" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4443333215152677949">I could say I wanted to love this book, but that would be a lie. <br/><br/>You know how some people feel <i>compelled</i> to finish a book, whether they like it or not? Well, I'm like that with series. Most of the time, at least.<br/><br/>Which is why I felt <i>compelled</i> to finish this book, even though I disliked Sweet Evil.<br/><br/>Here's just the general gist of what I hated:<br/>- <b>NOTHING EFFING HAPPENED! NADA!</b><br/>- TOO much obsessing over Kaidan on Anna's part.<br/>- Predictable plot- if you could even call it that.<br/>- Why was Kope even there? </span>
  <span id="freeText4443333215152677949" style="display:none">I could say I wanted to love this book, but that would be a lie. <br /><br />You know how some people feel <i>compelled</i> to finish a book, whether they like it or not? Well, I'm like that with series. Most of the time, at least.<br /><br />Which is why I felt <i>compelled</i> to finish this book, even though I disliked Sweet Evil.<br /><br />Here's just the general gist of what I hated:<br />- <b>NOTHING EFFING HAPPENED! NADA!</b><br />- TOO much obsessing over Kaidan on Anna's part.<br />- Predictable plot- if you could even call it that.<br />- Why was Kope even there? To assure Anna that Kaidan is "the one"?<br />- The ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the shooting scene <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was pretty much the same as the first book.<br />- Romance subplot takes front and center- I HATE it when books replace the actual plot with romance and call it a "plot". It's like the author couldn't think of a real story.<br /><br />I don't know how else to convince you of how utterly terrible this book is. But I will give you this: a character (who supposedly spoke perfect Spanish) said, <i><u>"Jugar</u> con mi chica?"</i><br /><br />Okay, anyone who has taken a <i>semester</i> of Spanish sees the fault in conjugation in that sentence. Sorry, Higgins, but just a tip: DON'T USE GOOGLE TRANSLATE.<br /><br />I know this is a small nitpick, but it annoyed me to no end and is a disgrace to all Spanish-speakers. <br /><br />Don't read this book. Just don't. It will only succeed in making you angry.<br /><br />One small tiny note: the kissing scenes were cute, I must admit, even if they got old after a while. Probably the only thing that stopped me from giving this book 1 star.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4443333215152677949" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16800629411444653205"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385184ra/744024.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/> <b> THAT WAS </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380385184ra/744025.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b> I LOVED IT!!! I love the way Wendy Higgins writes. When I read her books I am so into the book, I have no idea what is happening around me. I feel like I am in the book along with the other characters.<br/><br/>Another reason I love Wendy Higgins as a writer is because I feel the connection between the characters. I feel the love between Anna and Kaidan. It's like I can feel what Kopano is feeling towards Anna. I feel the protectiveness that Duke Belial has towards Anna.<br/><br/>I'm not very good wit</b></span>

I feel the protectiveness that Duke Belial has towards Anna.<br><br>I'm not very good with words so I wish that I could take all my feelings out of my heart and just copy and paste it to here. <br><br>I read Sweet Evil and had to wait a long time to get my hands on Sweet Peril. All those months eagerly awaiting the release and I finally got to finish it last night. It was magnetic, amazing and very exciting. Cant wait for the next book. Another 12 months of waiting and eagerly anticipating the release of Sweet Reckoning, the final book in the Sweet Trilogy Series. <br><br>I wish that Mrs Higgins would write a novella for each character. I would love to know a little bit more about Kopano, Ginger and Marna and Blake and most definantly Kaidan.<br><br>Anyway I 110% recommend this series.<br><br>Also everytime I read about Belial, this is who I picture. Every.Single.Bloody.Time. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385184i/744026.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br><br><br>July 24th 2012<br><b> COME ON HARPER TEEN PLEAAASSSEEEEE PUBLISH THIS BOOK I NEED TO HAVE IT NOW!!! Cant say I'm happy that its so far away, but im happy that at least its being published. Now we just have to wait *sigh*</span>
